### President inaugurates тАШGem Sri Lanka тАУ 2025тАЩ gem and jewellery exhibition

*2025-01-08 18:50:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104834/president-inaugurates-gem-sri-lanka-2025-gem-and-jewellery-exhibition) ┬╖ `en`

The тАЬGem Sri Lanka тАУ 2025тАЭ gem and jewellery exhibition was inaugurated this morning (08) at the Cinnamon Bentota Beach Hotel, presided over by President Anura Kumara Dissanayake.

Organized annually by the Chinese Fort Gem and Jewellery TradersтАЩ Association (CGJTA), the exhibition will be open to the public from today until January 10.

Following the opening, President Dissanayake toured the exhibition booths and engaged in discussions with industry stakeholders, addressing challenges faced by gem and jewellery manufacturers while fostering a friendly dialogue with them.

He also posed for a group photograph with the organizing committee of тАЬGem Sri Lanka тАУ 2025.тАЭ

This yearтАЩs exhibition features 103 booths and has attracted a significant number of both local and international buyers, highlighting the eventтАЩs global appeal.

р╢┤р╢╗р╖Кр╢║р╖Ър╖Вр╢л р╖Др╖П р╖Гр╢Вр╖Ар╢╗р╖Кр╢░р╢▒ р╖Ар╖Пр╢лр╖Тр╢вр╢Ър╢╗р╢л р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Ар╖Ър╖Бр╢║р╢Ър╖К р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П ┬аnirdc.gov.lk р╢▒р╖А р╖Ар╖Щр╢╢р╖К р╢Ер╢йр╖Ар╖Тр╢║ р╢пр╖Тр╢║р╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢п р╢╕р╖Щр╢╕ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖Ар╖Ъ р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Ф р╢Ър╖Щр╢╗р╖Тр╢лр╖Т.

р╢╕р╖Щр╖Др╖Тр╢пр╖У р╢Ер╢пр╖Др╖Гр╖К р╢пр╢Ър╖Кр╖Ар╢╕р╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢╕р╖Тр╢▒р╖Тр╖Гр╖Пр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Бр╖КтАНр╢║р╢нр╖П р╢▒р╖Ьр╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖Гр╖Кр╖А р╢┤р╖Ар╢нр╖Тр╢▒ р╢╢р╖А р╢┤р╖Щр╢▒р╖Кр╖Ар╖П р╢пр╖Фр╢▒р╖К р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢░р╖Тр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П, р╢Ср╢╕ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Бр╖КтАНр╢║р╢нр╖П р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢Ьр╢▒р╖Кр╢▒р╖П р╢╕р╖Пр╢пр╖Тр╢╜р╖Тр╢║ р╢┤р╢╕р╢лр╢Ър╖К р╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖Гр╖К р╖Ар╢▒ р╢╢р╖Ар╢п, р╢▒р╖А р╢Лр╢нр╖Кр╢┤р╖Пр╢пр╢▒р╢║ р╢нр╖Фр╖Ер╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢Ср╢╕ р╢╕р╖Пр╢пр╖Тр╢╜р╖Тр╢║ р╢▒р╖Тр╢╗р╖Кр╢╕р╖Пр╢лр╢║ р╢Ър╖Е р╖Др╖Рр╢Ър╖Т р╢╢р╖Ар╢п р╢Ър╖Тр╢║р╖П р╖Гр╖Тр╢зр╖Тр╢║р╖Ър╢║.

### Tens of thousands flee as wildfires tear through Los Angeles area

*2025-01-08 18:23:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104833/tens-of-thousands-flee-as-wildfires-tear-through-los-angeles-area) ┬╖ `en`

More than 30,000 people evacuated their homes as a wildfire ripped through an upscale coastal area of Los Angeles on Tuesday and into Wednesday, with Hollywood celebrities among those fleeing by car and on foot as flames engulfed homes and set hillsides ablaze.

Two other fires inland were also spreading fast, officials said.

Numerous buildings were destroyed and nearly 3,000 acres (1,200 hectares) burned in the Pacific Palisades area between the beach towns of Santa Monica and Malibu, officials said. The area is home to many film and music stars.

Roads were jammed with people fleeing the inferno, some abandoning their cars as flames licked the edges, and plumes of smoke and flames rose in the night sky over Los Angeles and its suburbs.

Firefighters has not contained the blaze by the early hours and Governor Gavin Newsom has declared a state of emergency.

р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢ор╖Ар╖Пр╖Др╢▒ р╢╕р╖Щр╖Др╖Щр╢║р╖Фр╢╕р╖К р╖Гр╢╕р╖Кр╢╢р╢▒р╖Кр╢░р╢║р╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╖Гр╖Д р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╢Ер╢нр╢╗ р╢Ер╢п (08р╢пр╖П) р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖Рр╢нр╖Т р╖Гр╖Пр╢Ър╢ар╖Кр╢бр╖Пр╖А р╖Гр╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢ор╢Ъ р╢╢р╖А р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К┬а р╢▒р╖Тр╢║р╖Ьр╢вр╖Тр╢нр╢║р╖Э р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╢нр╖Т.

р╢Т р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А, р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╖Ар╖Тр╖Гр╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╖Гр╖Рр╢╜р╖Гр╖Фр╢╕р╖К р╢Ър╖Е р╢пр╖Ур╢┤р╖Ар╖КтАНр╢║р╖Пр╢┤р╖Кр╢н р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Ар╢╗р╖Кр╢вр╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Ф р╢▒р╖Ьр╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢нр╖Ур╢╗р╢лр╢║ р╢Ър╖Е р╢╢р╖А р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖П р╢┤р╖Юр╢пр╖Кр╢Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╢Ъ р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Др╖Тр╢╕р╖Тр╢║р╢▒р╖Кр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╢║ р╢┤р╖Щр╢▒р╖Кр╖Ар╖П р╢пр╖Щр╢║р╖Т.

р╖Гр╖Тр╖Ар╖Тр╢╜р╖К р╢Зр╢│р╖Фр╢╕р╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╖Гр╖Рр╢╗р╖Гр╖Т р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╢▒р╖Тр╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖Ур╢▒р╖К р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢о р╢нр╖Фр╖Ер╢з р╢┤р╖Рр╢╕р╖Тр╢л р╢╗р╖Тр╢║р╢пр╖Фр╢╗р╖Ф р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╖Ар╖Рр╢╗р╢пр╖Т р╢▒р╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢Ър╖Кр╖Вр╢лр╢║ р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕ р╢╕р╖Др╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢Ер╢┤р╖Др╖Гр╖Фр╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╢║р╢з р╢┤р╢нр╖К р╢▒р╖Ьр╖Ар╢▒ р╢Жр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Щр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖Гр╖Ц р╢╢р╖Ар╢п р╢Ср╢╕ р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╢║р╖Ъ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╢┤р╢нр╖Т р╢Ьр╖Рр╢╕р╖Фр╢лр╖Ф р╖Ар╖Тр╢вр╖Ър╢╗р╢нр╖Кр╢▒ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖К р╢Ър╖Ер╖Ър╢║.

р╢╕р╖Ур╢з р╢Ер╢╕р╢нр╢╗р╖А р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢о р╢нр╖Фр╖Е р╖Гр╖Ар╖Тр╢Ър╢╗ р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Щр╢▒ р╢Ер╢╕р╢нр╢╗ р╢Лр╢┤р╖Пр╢Вр╢Ь р╢Йр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢╕р╖Пр╖Г р╢нр╖Фр╢▒р╢Ъ р╖Гр╖Др╢▒ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║р╢Ър╖Кр╢п р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢пр╖Фр╢▒р╖К р╢╢р╖Ар╢п р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖Гр╖Ур╢║.

р╖Ар╖Рр╢╗р╢пр╖Т р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╗р╖Тр╢║р╢пр╖Фр╢╗р╢▒р╖Кр╢з р╢▒р╖Ур╢нр╖Тр╢║ р╢Ър╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Тр╢║р╖Пр╢нр╖Кр╢╕р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Е р╢║р╖Фр╢нр╖Ф р╢╢р╖Ар╢нр╖К, р╢Ср╖Др╖Щр╢нр╖К р╢Ер╢пр╖Пр╖Е р╢Ър╢зр╢║р╖Фр╢нр╖Фр╖Ар╢╜р╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢╕р╖Др╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢Ер╢┤р╖Др╖Гр╖Фр╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╢║р╢з р╢┤р╢нр╖К р╢▒р╖Ьр╖Ар╖Тр╢║ р╢║р╖Фр╢нр╖Ф р╢╢р╖Ар╢п р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖К р╢Ър╖Ер╖Ър╢║.

### р╢╕р╖Пр╖Ер╖Ф р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╖К р╢Ьр╖Щр╢йр╖Тр╢║р╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢╕р╢нр╖Ф р╖Ар╖Ц р╢╜р╢║р╖Тр╢зр╢╗р╖К р╢Ър╖Ср╢╜р╖Т

*2025-01-08 18:01:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanasinhalalk`](http://sinhala.adaderana.lk/news/205181) ┬╖ `si`

р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╢пр╖Фр╢╗ р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Кр╢░ р╖Др╖Эр╢зр╢╜р╢║р╢Ър╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢╕р╖Тр╢╜ р╢пр╖У р╢Ьр╢нр╖К р╢╕р╖Пр╖Ер╖Ф р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╖К р╢Ьр╖Щр╢йр╖Тр╢║р╢Ъ┬ар╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖У р╢╜р╢║р╖Тр╢зр╢╗р╢║р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Ьр╢зр╖Гр╖К р╖Др╢╕р╖Фр╖А р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Ъ.

р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╢пр╖Фр╢╗ р╢Ер╢╗р╖Фр╢Ър╖Кр╢Ьр╖Ьр╢й р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╢пр╖Ър╖Бр╢║р╖Ъ р╢┤р╢пр╖Тр╢Вр╢ар╖Т р╢╕р╢Вр╢вр╖Фр╢╜ р╢┤р╖Щр╢╗р╖Ър╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П р╢Ер╢п (08) р╢Лр╢пр╖Ср╖Гр╢▒ р╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╢┤р╖Фр╢нр╖Фр╢▒р╖К р╢пр╖Щр╢пр╖Щр╢▒р╖Пр╢з р╢╜р╢╢р╖Пр╢пр╖Ур╢╕ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢Ер╢пр╖Пр╖Е р╖Др╖Эр╢зр╢╜р╢║р╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢╕р╖Пр╖Ер╖Ф р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╖К р╢Ьр╖Щр╢йр╖Т р╢пр╖Щр╢Ър╢Ър╖К р╢╕р╖Тр╖Ер╢пр╖У р╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒ р╢Зр╢н.

р╢Ср╖Др╖Тр╢пр╖У, р╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╢╢р╖Пр╢╜ р╢┤р╖Фр╢нр╖Ф р╢Ър╖Ср╢╕ р╢Ьр╢нр╖К р╢╕р╖Пр╖Ер╖Ф р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╖К р╢Ьр╖Щр╢йр╖Тр╢║р╖Ъ┬ар╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖У р╢╜р╢║р╖Тр╢зр╢╗р╢║р╢Ъ р╢╜р╖Эр╖Др╢╕р╢║ р╢Ър╖Ьр╢зр╖Гр╢Ър╖К р╖Др╢╕р╖Фр╖А р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Ъ.

р╢Т р╢╕р╖Ьр╖Др╖Ьр╢нр╖Ър╢╕ р╢╕р╢Вр╢вр╖Фр╢╜ р╢┤р╖Щр╢╗р╖Ър╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╢пр╖Ър╖Бр╢║ р╢╖р╖Пр╢╗ р╢╕р╖Др╢вр╢▒ р╖Гр╖Юр╢Ыр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢┤р╢╗р╖Ур╢Ър╖Кр╖Вр╢Ър╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖Пр╖А р╢╕р╖Ъ р╢╢р╖А р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╖Фр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Зр╢нр╢нр╖К р╢Фр╖Др╖Ф р╢┤р╖Ар╖Гр╖П р╢Зр╢нр╖Кр╢нр╖Ъ, р╢Ер╢п р╢пр╖Тр╢▒р╢║р╖Ъ р╢нр╢╕р╢▒р╖К р╢▒р╖Тр╖Ар╖Пр╢йр╖Ф р╢╢р╖Ар╢нр╖К, р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╢пр╖Фр╢╗ р╖Гр╖Юр╢Ыр╖КтАНр╢║ р╖Ар╖Ыр╢пр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢▒р╖Тр╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖У р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢║р╖Пр╢╜р╢║ р╖Ар╖Щр╢н р╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢зр╢╜р╖Фр╖А р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╖Фр╢╕р╖Кр╢пр╖Щр╢▒ р╢╜р╖Щр╖Гр╢нр╖Кр╢║.

р╢Т р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╢пр╖Фр╢╗ р╖Гр╖Юр╢Ыр╖КтАНр╢║ р╖Ар╖Ыр╢пр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢▒р╖Тр╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖У р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢║р╖Пр╢╜р╢║ р╖Ар╖Щр╢н р╢Ьр╖Ьр╖Гр╖К р╢╕р╖Ъ р╢╢р╖А р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖Гр╖Фр╖Ар╢п р╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╢┤р╖Рр╢╕р╖Тр╢лр╖Тр╢╜р╖Кр╢╜ р╢╖р╖Пр╢╗ р╢▒р╖Ьр╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒ р╢нр╢╕р╢▒р╖Кр╖А р╢Жр╢┤р╖Гр╖Ф р╖Др╢╗р╖Ар╖П р╢Ср╖Ар╖Ц р╢╢р╖А р╢╕р╢Вр╢вр╖Фр╢╜ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П р╢┤р╖Ар╖Гр╢║р╖Т.

р╢Ср╢╕р╖Щр╢▒р╖Кр╢╕ р╢Фр╖Др╖Фр╢з р╢Ср╖Др╖Тр╢пр╖У р╢▒р╖Тр╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖Ур╢▒р╖К р╢┤р╖Ар╖Гр╖П р╢Зр╢нр╖Кр╢нр╖Ъ р╢Ср╢╕ р╖Др╖Эр╢зр╢╜р╢║ р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒р╢пр╖Фр╢╗ р╢▒р╢Ьр╢╗ р╖Гр╢╖р╖П р╖Гр╖Ур╢╕р╖Пр╖Ар╖Ъ р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╖Др╖Эр╢зр╢╜р╢║р╢Ър╖К р╢╢р╖Рр╖Ар╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢Т р╖Гр╢╕р╖Кр╢╢р╢▒р╖Кр╢░р╢║р╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢▒р╢Ьр╢╗ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╢║р╖Фр╢Ър╖Кр╢н р╢╕р╖Др╢вр╢▒ р╖Гр╖Юр╢Ыр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢┤р╢╗р╖Ур╢Ър╖Кр╖Вр╢Ър╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖Пр╢з р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╖Фр╢╕р╖К р╢пр╖Щр╢▒ р╢╜р╖Щр╖Гр╢║.

### Japan's assistance to resume temporarily parked projects

*2025-01-08 17:48:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanasinhalalk`](http://sinhala.adaderana.lk/news/205180) ┬╖ `si`

Japan aids restarting suspended projects in Sri Lanka. Japanese Ambassador discusses resuming temporarily halted projects & accelerating airport terminal construction. Long-term ties between nations strengthen development efforts.

ЁЯЯй

Japanese Ambassador, Ambassador, Ambassador to Sri Lanka, says that the government is discussing temporarily parked projects in Sri Lanka.

He was speaking at a meeting of Speaker Jagath Wickramaratne in Parliament recently.

The Japanese Ambassador also said that the construction of the new terminal at the Bandaranaike International Airport was also expected to be expedited.

The Japanese Ambassador who recalled on the long-term relationship between Sri Lanka and he further stated that the development of Sri Lanka is further strengthened.

The Japanese Ambassador has joined the government, including the Speaker,.

The Speaker, the Speaker, recalled the projects that the Japanese government had given to the people of this country to Japan.

The Speaker said that the Third Parliament is expected to re-establish the Sri Lanka-Japan Parliamentary Association to strengthen relations between the two countries.

### р╖Ар╖Щр╖Ер╢│ р╖Др╖П р╢║р╖Фр╢п р╢▒р╖Юр╢Ър╖П р╖Гр╖Тр╢║р╢╜р╖Кр╢╜р╢╕ р╢Ср╢▒р╖Кр╢▒р╖Ъ р╢вр╖Пр╢нр╖КтАНр╢║р╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╢╗ р╖Гр╢╕р╖Кр╢╕р╖Фр╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╜р╢з р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖Ар╢║р╖Т

р╢Ср╖Др╖Тр╢пр╖У р╢Т р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╢╗р╢зр╢нр╖К р╢Ер╖Ар╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╢лр╢║ р╢Ър╢╗ р╖Гр╖Тр╢зр╖Тр╢║р╖Ъ, р╢Ср╢╕ р╢║р╖Фр╢п р╢Ер╢╖р╖КтАНр╢║р╖Пр╖Г р╖Бр╖КтАНр╢╗р╖У р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖П р╢▒р╖Пр╖Ар╖Тр╢Ъ р╖Др╢╕р╖Фр╢пр╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╢╕р╖Щр╢▒р╖Кр╢╕, р╖Ар╖Щр╢╗р╖Ер╖Пр╢╗р╢Ър╖Кр╖Вр╢Ъ р╢пр╖Щр╢┤р╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢нр╢╕р╖Ър╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╖Фр╖Ар╢з р╢╕р╖Фр╖Др╖Фр╢п р╖Др╢╗р╖Др╖П р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢вр╖Пр╢нр╖КтАНр╢║р╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╢╗ р╢╕р╢нр╖Кр╢пр╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Ар╖КтАНр╢║ р╢вр╖Пр╖Ар╖Пр╢╗р╢╕ р╢╕р╖Рр╢мр╢╜р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖К р╢Лр╢┤р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖У р╖Ар╢▒ р╢╢р╖Ар╢║р╖Т.

р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢ор╖Ар╢╜ р╢Ер╢▒р╖Ар╖Бр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢Ер╢╕р╢нр╢╗ р╢Лр╢┤р╖Пр╢Вр╢Ь р╢Йр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢┤р╖Юр╢пр╖Кр╢Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╢Ъ р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Др╖Тр╢╕р╖Тр╢║р╢▒р╖Кр╢з р╢╕р╖Пр╖Г р╢нр╖Фр╢▒р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║р╢Ър╖К р╢╜р╢╢р╖Пр╢пр╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢нр╖Ур╢╗р╢лр╢║ р╢Ър╖Е р╢╢р╖А р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╢╕р╖Пр╢░р╖КтАНр╢║ р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╢Ър╖Пр╖Бр╢Ъ, р╢вр╖КтАНр╢║р╖Щр╖Вр╖Кр╢и р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╢Ер╢░р╖Тр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Т р╢╢р╖Фр╢пр╖Кр╢░р╖Тр╢Ъ р╢╕р╢▒р╢нр╖Фр╢Вр╢Ь р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖Гр╖Ур╢║.

р╢┤р╖Юр╢пр╖Кр╢Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╢Ъ р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢о р╖Др╖Тр╢╕р╖Тр╢║р╢▒р╖Кр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╖Гр╖Д р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Т р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Тр╢║р╢▒р╖Кр╢н р╖Ар╖Ур╢╗р╖Гр╖Цр╢╗р╖Тр╢║ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П р╢Ер╢нр╢╗ р╢Ер╢п (8) р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖Рр╢нр╖К р╖Ар╖Ц р╖Гр╖Пр╢Ър╢ар╖Кр╢бр╖Пр╖Ар╖Ър╢пр╖У р╢╕р╖Щр╢╕ р╢нр╖Ур╢╗р╢лр╢║р╢з р╢┤р╖Рр╢╕р╖Тр╢лр╖Т р╢╢р╖А р╖Др╖Щр╢нр╖Щр╢╕ р╢┤р╖Ар╖Гр╢║р╖Т.

р╢╕р╖Щр╢╕ р╖Гр╖Пр╢Ър╢ар╖Кр╢бр╖Пр╖Ар╖Ър╢пр╖У р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╢┤р╖Ар╖Гр╖П р╢Зр╢нр╖Кр╢нр╖Ъ р╢╗р╢зр╢Ъ р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢Ь р╖Ар╖Тр╢▒р╢║ р╢║р╢▒р╖Ф р╢╗р╢зр╢Ъ р╢нр╢нр╖Кр╢нр╖Кр╖Ар╢║ р╢┤р╖Тр╖Ер╖Тр╢╢р╢│ р╢╕р╖Тр╢▒р╖Фр╢╕р╖К р╢пр╢лр╖Кр╢йр╢║р╢Ър╖К р╢╢р╖Ар╢║.

р╢Т р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А р╢пр╖Ър╖Бр╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒ р╢Ер╢нр╢Ьр╖Рр╖Гр╖Ур╢╕р╖Кр╖Ар╢╜р╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢нр╖Ьр╢╗р╖А р╢╕р╖Ъ р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖Тр╢з р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢Ь р╖Ар╖Тр╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╢Ър╖Гр╖Кр╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╖Ъ р╢Ър╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Тр╢║р╖Пр╖Ар╢╜р╖Тр╢║ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢┤р╖Ар╢нр╖Кр╢▒р╖П р╢▒р╖Ур╢нр╖Т р╢Лр╢┤р╢║р╖Эр╢Ьр╖У р╢Ър╢╗р╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒ р╢╕р╖Щр╖Др╖Щр╢║р╖Фр╢╕р╖К р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╢р╖А р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╖Фр╢╕р╖К р╢пр╖У р╢Зр╢н.

### Bus strike called off after talks with police chief

*2025-01-08 17:06:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104832/bus-strike-called-off-after-talks-with-police-chief) ┬╖ `en`

The bus associations have decided to call off their island-wide strike following successful discussions with the Acting IGP.

This decision was reached after a successful discussion held today (08) between the private bus associations and the Acting Inspector General of Police (IGP), Priyantha Weerasooriya, regarding traffic operations linked to the тАШClean Sri LankaтАЩ national initiative.

As a result, the bus associations have decided to call off their planned island-wide strike.

Earlier, the bus associations had decided yesterday (07) to launch an island-wide strike to protest against the police departmentтАЩs excessive and unnecessary pressure on passenger transport bus operators.

In this context, representatives from the bus associations held a discussion with the Acting Inspector General of Police (IGP), Priyantha Weerasooriya, at the Police Headquarters this morning (08).

### р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╢Йр╢╜р╖Кр╢╜р╖Ур╢╕р╖К р╢пр╖Щр╢Ър╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢Ср╢Ър╢Ър╢з р╖Ар╖Р.р╢╢. р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖А

*2025-01-08 16:51:25* ┬╖ [`adalk`](https://www.ada.lk/breaking_news/р╢╢р╖Гр╖К-р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К-р╢Йр╢╜р╖Кр╢╜р╖Ур╢╕р╖К-р╢пр╖Щр╢Ър╖Щр╢▒р╖К-р╢Ср╢Ър╢Ър╢з-р╖Ар╖Р-р╢╢--р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╢Ьр╖Ъ-р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖А/11-414096) ┬╖ `si`

р╢Ър╖Кр╢╜р╖Ур╢▒р╖К р╖Бр╖КтАНр╢╗р╖У р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖П р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Гр╢зр╖Др╢▒р╢з р╖Гр╢╕р╢Ьр╖Пр╢╕р╖Ур╖А р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢Ь р╢Ер╢▒р╢нр╖Фр╢╗р╖Ф р╢Ер╖Ар╢╕ р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒р╖Ур╢╕ р╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖Фр╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Ур╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╢Ър╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Тр╢║р╖Пр╢нр╖Кр╢╕р╢Ъ р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╗р╢о р╖Ар╖Пр╖Др╢▒ р╢╕р╖Щр╖Др╖Щр╢║р╖Фр╢╕ р╖Др╖П р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╢▒р╖Тр╢║р╖Эр╢вр╖Тр╢нр╢║р╢▒р╖К р╢Ер╢нр╢╗ р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖Рр╢нр╖Т р╖Гр╖Пр╢Ър╢ар╖Кр╢бр╖Пр╖Ар╖Ър╢пр╖У р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╢Йр╢пр╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╢┤р╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Е р╢Ср╢Ър╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╖Фр╢лр╢Ър╢з р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢╜р╖Рр╢╢р╖У р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢Ер╢нр╢╗ р╢нр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╖Фр╢лр╢Ър╢з р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢пр╢Ър╖Кр╖Ар╖П р╢▒р╖Ьр╢╕р╖Рр╢н.

р╢╕р╖Щр╖Др╖Тр╢пр╖У р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢ор╖Ар╢╜ р╢Ер╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╢╗р╢лр╢║р╢з р╖Гр╢Ър╖Гр╖К р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢пр╖С р╖Др╖П р╢Тр╖Ар╖П р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╢Ер╢▒р╢нр╖Фр╢╗р╖Фр╖Ар╢╜р╢з р╢нр╖Фр╢йр╖Ф┬атАНр╢▒р╖Ьр╢пр╖Щр╢▒р╖Кр╢▒р╖Ър╢▒р╢╕р╖К р╢┤р╢╕р╢лр╢Ър╖К р╢Тр╖Ар╖П р╢Йр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢╕р╖Пр╖Г р╢нр╖Фр╢▒р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║р╢Ър╖К р╢╜р╢╢р╖Пр╢пр╖Щр╢▒ р╢╜р╖Щр╖Гр╢з р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢о р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╢▒р╖Тр╢║р╖Эр╢вр╢нр╢║р╢▒р╖К р╢Ър╖Е р╢Йр╢╜р╖Кр╢╜р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╖Ар╖Рр╢й р╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖Пр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢╜р╖Рр╢╢р╖У р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Ъ.

р╢Т р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А р╢Ер╢пр╖Пр╖Е р╖Гр╖Рр╢╗р╖Гр╖Тр╢╜р╖Т р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╢Ер╢▒р╢нр╖Фр╢╗р╖Фр╖Ар╢╜р╢з р╖Др╖Ър╢нр╖Ф р╖Ар╢▒р╖Кр╢▒р╖Ъ р╢▒р╢╕р╖К р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╢╕р╖Рр╢пр╖Тр╖Др╢нр╖Кр╖Ар╖У р╢Тр╖Ар╖П р╢Йр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢Ър╢зр╢║р╖Фр╢нр╖Ф р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒р╖Ф р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢╢р╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ер╢▒р╖Щр╢Ър╖Фр╢нр╖К р╢пр╖С р╢Йр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╖Др╖Э р╢▒р╖Тр╖Гр╖Т р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╢╗ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒ р╢╗р╢│р╖Ар╖Пр╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒ р╢нр╢╢р╖П р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒р╖Ур╢╕ р╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖Фр╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢╕р╖Пр╖Г р╢нр╖Фр╢▒р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║р╢Ър╖К р╢╜р╢╢р╖Пр╢пр╖Щр╢▒ р╢╢р╖А р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖К р╢Ър╢╗ р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Ъ.

р╢╕р╖Ъ р╢Ер╢нр╢╗ р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╢╗р╢ор╖Ар╢╜ р╖Ар╖Рр╢╗р╢пр╖Т р╖Гр╖Щр╖Ар╖Ур╢╕ р╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖Фр╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╖Гр╖Тр╖Ар╖Тр╢╜р╖К р╢Зр╢│р╖Фр╢╕р╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢║р╖Ьр╢пр╖Ар╖П р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╢▒р╖Тр╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖Ур╢▒р╖К р╢Йр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╜р╖Щр╖Гр╢з р╢╢р╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╢╕р╖К р╢Ър╖Е р╢Йр╢╜р╖Кр╢╜р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╖Ар╖Рр╢й р╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖Пр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢╜р╖Рр╢╢р╖У р╢▒р╖Ьр╢╕р╖Рр╢н. р╢╕р╖Др╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╢Ьр╖Ъ р╢Жр╢╗р╢Ър╖Кр╖Вр╖Пр╖А р╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖Фр╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢Ср╢║ р╢Ер╢Ыр╢лр╖Кр╢йр╖А р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╖Ар╖Рр╢й р╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖Кр╢┤р╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖К р╢Ър╢╗ р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Ъ.

### IGP orders probe into over 1,000 candidates over election expenditure violations

*2025-01-08 16:33:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104831/igp-orders-probe-into-over-1000-candidates-over-election-expenditure-violations) ┬╖ `en`

The Acting Inspector General of Police (IGP) has ordered an investigation into 1,042 candidates and 197 party secretaries and independent group leaders who failed to report their income and expenditure for the 2024 general election, in violation of the Regulation of Election Expenditure Act.

Under the Election Expenditure Regulation Act, No. 03 of 2023, all political parties, independent groups, or candidates are required to submit their financial reports to the District Returning Officers within 21 days of the election results being announced.

Accordingly, Acting IGP Priyantha Weerasooriya has instructed police divisions in the relevant electoral districts to begin investigations.

Additionally, the police chief has ordered all Senior DIGs, DIGs, and Divisional Officers to prepare reports on these investigations and submit them to the Attorney General for legal advice by January 31, 2025.

...

### Sri Lanka stocks up for first time in four sessions; banks lead

*2025-01-08 16:19:00* ┬╖ [`economynextcom`](https://economynext.com/sri-lanka-stocks-up-for-first-time-in-four-sessions-banks-lead-198591/) ┬╖ `en`

ECONOMYNEXT тАУ The Colombo Stock Exchange indices rose on Wednesday, bucking a falling trend in the last three sessions, data on its site showed.

Market has been on the downward trend for the past three sessions through Tuesday after peaking repeatedly following the finalization of Sri LankaтАЩs debt restructuring deal in mid December.

The broader ASPI closed up 0.63 percent or 99.37 points at 15,954.01; while the more liquid S&P SL20 Index closed up 0.57 percent or 27.12 points at 4,816.10.

тАЬRenewed buying interest is pushing the market up,тАЭ Dimantha Mathew, Chief Research & Strategy Officer at First Capital Holdings PLC, told EconomyNext.

тАЬWe saw short profit taking in the last three days, but the upward trend will continueтАЭ he said referring to the market recovery.

Analysts say more investors are shifting their money to stocks from fixed-income assets after President Anura Kumara Dissanayake doubled withholding tax on interest income. Returns on stock investments are tax free.

р╢┤р╢╜р╖Пр╢Ьр╖Тр╢║ р╢Зр╢нр╖Рр╢╕р╖К р╢┤р╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╢╗р╢ор╖Ар╖Пр╖Др╢▒ р╢┤р╖Ар╖П р╢Ер╢нр╖Кр╖Др╖Рр╢╗ р╢пр╢╕р╖Пр╢Ьр╖Ьр╖Гр╖К р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢Ер╢нр╢╗, р╢Ср╢╜р╖Щр╖Г р╢Ер╢нр╖Кр╖Др╖Рр╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Тр╢║ р╢╗р╢ор╖Ар╖Пр╖Др╢▒ р╖Др╖Ър╢нр╖Фр╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢Зр╢нр╖Тр╖Ар╖Ц р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢Ь р╢Ер╖Ар╖Др╖Тр╢╗р╢нр╖П р╢Йр╖Ар╢нр╖Кр╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢╢р╖Рр╢Ър╖Э р╢║р╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╖КтАНр╢╗ р╢║р╖Ьр╢пр╖Пр╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒р╖Ур╢╕р╢зр╢нр╖К р╢п р╢╢р╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖Ур╢▒р╖Кр╢з р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Фр╖А р╢Зр╢н.

### Sri Lanka cabinet approves MOUs with Chinese media institutions for training

*2025-01-08 15:29:00* ┬╖ [`economynextcom`](https://economynext.com/sri-lanka-cabinet-approves-mous-with-chinese-media-institutions-for-training-198594/) ┬╖ `en`

ECONOMYNEXT тАУ Sri LankaтАЩs cabinet this week approved proposals to enter into agreements with Chinese media institutions for capacity building ahead of President Anura Kumara DissanayakeтАЩs January 14 official visit to Beijing.

The signing of the memorandum of understanding (MOU) will see Sri Lanka officials from the Ministry and Department of Government Information as well as journalists from state media institutions going to China for capacity building through training, a government official said.

The Ministry of Health and Mass Media will sign an MOU with National Radio and Television Administration (NRTA) of China, while the Associated Newspapers Ceylon Limited (Lake House) will sign with Chinese state-owned Xinhua News Agency.

Similarly, the Department of Government Information will sign with Xinhua News Agency, while state-run Sri Lanka Rupavahini Corporation and Sri Lanka Broadcasting Corporation will sign the MOU with China Media Group.

р╢Ср╢╕ р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╢пр╖Ър╖Бр╢║р╖Ъ р╢йр╖Ьр╢╜р╖Кр╖Жр╖Тр╢▒р╖Кр╢╕р╢нр╖Кр╖Гр╖КтАНр╢║р╢║р╢▒р╖К ┬а11р╢Ър╖Ф р╢╕р╖Тр╢║ р╢Ьр╖Щр╖Пр╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╖Тр╢зр╖Тр╢║ р╢пр╖У р╢╕р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Кр╢╜р╖Тр╢Ър╖Фр╢╜р╢╕ р╢Ер╢йр╖Ар╖Т р╢Жр╢╗р╢Ър╖Кр╖Вр╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢║р╖Пр╢╜р╢║р╖Ъ р╢▒р╖Тр╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖Ур╢▒р╖К р╢┤р╖Гр╖Фр╢Ьр╖Тр╢║р╢пр╖П р╖Гр╖Ьр╢║р╖П р╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒ р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Ц р╢Ер╢нр╢╗, р╢Т р╢┤р╖Тр╖Ер╖Тр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╢Кр╢║р╖Ъ (07) р╢┤р╖Фр╢нр╖Кр╢нр╢╜р╢╕ р╢╕р╖Др╖Ър╖Гр╖Кр╢нр╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Пр╢нр╖К р╢Ер╢░р╖Тр╢Ър╢╗р╢лр╢║р╢з р╢Ър╢╗р╖Фр╢лр╖Ф р╢Йр╢пр╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╢┤р╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╖Ар╢▒р╢вр╖Ур╖Ар╖Т р╢▒р╖Тр╢╜р╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╖Ур╢▒р╖К р╢┤р╖Тр╢║р╖Ар╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒ р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢╢р╖Ар╢п р╢Ср╢╕ р╢пр╖Щр╢┤р╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢нр╢╕р╖Ър╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╖Фр╖А р╢Ър╖Тр╢║р╢║р╖Т.

р╢╕р╖Щр╢╕ р╖Гр╢нр╖Фр╢▒р╖Кр╢Ьр╖Ъ р╢╕р╢╗р╢л р╢┤р╢╗р╖Ур╢Ър╖Кр╖Вр╢лр╢║ р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╢╗р╖Пр╢░р╢┤р╖Фр╢╗ р╖Ар╢▒р╢вр╖Ур╖Ар╖Т р╢┤р╖Бр╖Ф р╖Ар╖Ыр╢пр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢║р╖Пр╢╜р╢║р╖Ъ р╢ар╢▒р╖Кр╢пр╢▒ р╢вр╢║р╖Гр╖Тр╢Вр╖Д р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П р╖Гр╖Д р╢йр╢╢р╖Кр╢╜р╖Тр╖Ар╖К. р╢Ср╢╜р╖К. р╢║р╖Ц. р╢╕р╢░р╖Фр╖Ар╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╖Т р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖Кр╢╕р╖Тр╢║ р╢║р╢▒ р╖Ар╢▒р╢вр╖Ур╖Ар╖Т р╢┤р╖Бр╖Ф р╖Ар╖Ыр╢пр╖КтАНр╢║р╖Ар╢╗р╖Фр╢▒р╖К р╖Ар╖Тр╖Гр╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╖Гр╖Тр╢пр╖Ф р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╜р╢п р╢╢р╖Ар╢нр╖К, р╢Ср╢╕ р╖Гр╢нр╖Фр╢▒р╖К р╢пр╖Рр╢╜р╢Ъ р╢┤р╖Рр╢зр╢╜р╖Ур╢╕ р╖Др╖Ър╢нр╖Фр╖Ар╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢╕р╢╗р╢лр╢║р╢з р╢┤р╢нр╖Кр╖А р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╢╕р╖Пр╢▒ р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒р╖Ф р╢╜р╢╢р╢▒ р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢▒р╖Тр╢╗р╖Кр╢пр╖Ър╖Б р╢Ър╖Ьр╢з р╢Зр╢нр╖Рр╢║р╖Т р╖Ар╢▒р╢вр╖Ур╖Ар╖Тр╢пр╖Щр╢┤р╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢нр╢╕р╖Ър╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╖Фр╖Ар╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╢║р╖Т.

### Sri LankaтАЩs central bank to focus on stronger crisis recovery in 2025

*2025-01-08 15:16:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104830/sri-lankas-central-bank-to-focus-on-stronger-crisis-recovery-in-2025) ┬╖ `en`

Sri Lanka will focus on stronger recovery this year after the island nation posted real GDP growth of 5% in 2024, the highest in seven years, its central bank chief said on Wednesday, hoping to accelerate a rebound from its worst financial crisis in decades.

Sri LankaтАЩs economy crumpled under a severe foreign exchange crisis in 2022, but has posted a faster than expected rally after it secured a $2.9 billion International Monetary Fund (IMF) program in March 2023 and completed a $25 billion debt restructuring in December.

The economy grew 5.2% in the first nine months of 2024, outstripping the 3% estimate by the Central Bank of Sri Lanka (CBSL), Governor P. Nandalal Weerasinghe said.

тАЬAchieving a transformative acceleration in growth trajectory is essential to catch up and enhance the growth potential. This would also help enhance the debt-carrying capacity of the country,тАЭ he said at an annual policy agenda launch.

*2025-01-08 15:14:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanasinhalalk`](http://sinhala.adaderana.lk/news/205171) ┬╖ `si`

р╢╗р╖Фр╖Гр╖Тр╢║р╖Пр╖А р╖Гр╖Д р╢Фр╢┤р╖Щр╢Ър╖К р╖Гр╖Пр╢╕р╖Пр╢вр╖Тр╢Ъ р╢╗р╢зр╖Ар╢╜р╖К р╖Гр╖Тр╢║ р╖Гр╖Рр╢┤р╢║р╖Фр╢╕р╖К р╖Гр╖Ур╢╕р╖П р╢Ър╖Тр╢╗р╖Ур╢╕ р╢Кр╢з р╢Ср╢Ър╖К р╖Др╖Ър╢нр╖Фр╖Ар╢Ър╖К р╢╜р╖Щр╖Г р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖Кр╢║.

р╢Т р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А р╢╢р╖КтАНр╢╗р╖Щр╢▒р╖Кр╢зр╖К р╢╢р╖Ьр╢╗р╢нр╖Щр╢╜р╖К р╢╢р╖Рр╢╗р╢╜р╢║р╢Ъ р╢╕р╖Тр╢╜ р╖Гр╖Тр╢║р╢║р╢з 0.42р╢Ър╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢йр╖Ьр╢╜р╢╗р╖К 77.37 р╢пр╢Ър╖Кр╖Ар╖П р╢п р╖Ар╖Щр╖Гр╖Кр╢зр╖К р╢зр╖Щр╢Ър╖Кр╖Гр╖Пр╖Гр╖К р╢╢р╖Ьр╢╗р╢нр╖Щр╢╜р╖К р╢╢р╖Рр╢╗р╢╜р╢║р╢Ъ р╢╕р╖Тр╢╜ р╖Гр╖Тр╢║р╢║р╢з 0.57р╢Ър╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢йр╖Ьр╢╜р╢╗р╖К 74.67р╢Ър╖К р╢пр╢Ър╖Кр╖Ар╖П р╢п р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Т р╖Ар╖У р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Фр╢лр╖Т.

р╢Т р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А р╢нр╢╗р╢Ь 3р╢Ър╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢║р╖Фр╢нр╖К р╢╕р╖Щр╢╕ р╢нр╢╗р╢Ьр╖Пр╖Ар╢╜р╖Тр╢║р╖Ъ р╢нр╖Ар╢нр╖К р╢нр╢╗р╢Ьр╢║р╢Ър╖К р╢Йр╢нр╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╖А р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Тр╢║р╢пр╖Ур╢╕ р╢нр╢╗р╢Ьр╖Пр╖Ар╢╜р╖Тр╢║р╖Ъ р╢вр╢║ р╢нр╖Др╖Ар╖Фр╢╗р╖Ф р╢Ър╢╗р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒р╖Ур╢╕р╢з р╢▒р╖Ар╖Гр╖Ур╢╜р╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╢║р╢з р╖Др╖Рр╢Ър╖Тр╖Ар╖Тр╢║.

### President appoints new High Commissioner and four Ambassadors

*2025-01-08 14:34:40* ┬╖ [`dailyftlk`](https://www.ft.lk/news/President-appoints-new-High-Commissioner-and-four-Ambassadors/56-771576) ┬╖ `en`

New diplomats urged to promote image of country on international arena

Calls for strengthening bilateral ties and enhancing migrant worker welfare

President Anura Kumara Disanayake yesterday appointed a High Commissioner and four Ambassadors to serve in Sri LankaтАЩs diplomatic service.

The newly appointed representatives include: Ambassador-designate to Qatar R.S. Khan Azard, High Commissioner-designate for New Zealand W.G.S. Prasanna, Ambassador-designate for Russia S.K. Gunasekera, Ambassador-designate for Kuwait L.P. Ratnayaka, and Ambassador-designate for Egypt A. S. K. Seneviratne.

The newly designated diplomats also engaged in a brief discussion with the President following the appointments.

President Disanayake expressed his confidence in the newly appointed diplomats, emphasising the importance of their roles in strengthening Sri LankaтАЩs bilateral ties and fostering mutual cooperation with the respective nations.

### Sri Lanka central bank to review SRR framework

*2025-01-08 14:05:00* ┬╖ [`economynextcom`](https://economynext.com/sri-lanka-central-bank-to-review-srr-framework-198588/) ┬╖ `en`

ECONOMYNEXT тАУ Sri LankaтАЩs central bank is reviewing the current statutory reserve requirements of banks, Governor Nandalal Weeerasinghe said delivering the agencyтАЩs annual plans for the year.

The central bank is reviewing the SRR in line with international best practices, he said.

тАЬRequired changes will be implemented following stakeholder consultations to optimise the SRR framework for the benefit of effective monetary policy implementation and the overall financial system,тАЭ according to the published text of the speech.

Many floating rate central banks no longer have large reserve requirements, and do not use them to tighten or loosen policy.

The Fed in the run up to triggering the latest inflation bubble, dropped the concept of required reserves altogether.

It could then print money without the limits of тАШexcess reserves or excess liquidityтАЩ, critics say.

тАЬHowever, the Central Bank observes some excessive, outlier rates of interest on facilities extended to Micro, Small and Medium Scale Enterprises (MSMEs) as well as marginal borrowers and certain credit products, which are not consistent with the prevailing relaxed monetary policy stance,тАЭ he said.

тАЬBut I can say this, we need them for economic security,тАЭ he told reporters during a wide-ranging news conference at his Mar-a-Lago estate in Florida.

Both Denmark and Panama have rejected any suggestion that they would give up territory.

Trump also vowed to use тАЬeconomic forceтАЭ when asked if he would attempt to annex Canada and called their shared border an тАЬartificially drawn lineтАЭ.

The boundary is the worldтАЩs longest between two countries and it was established in treaties dating back to the founding of the US in the late 1700s.

### Sri LankaтАЩs 2024 GDP growth hits 7-year high of 5-pct amid deflation

*2025-01-08 13:00:00* ┬╖ [`economynextcom`](https://economynext.com/sri-lankas-2024-gdp-growth-hits-7-year-high-of-5-pct-198582/) ┬╖ `en`

ECONOMYNEXT тАУ Sri LankaтАЩs economy is estimated to have expanded by 5 percent last year and recorded the highest growth since 2017, the Central Bank Governor Nandalal Weerasinghe said.

Announcing the policy agenda for 2025 and beyond he said leading economic indicators of industry and service sectors reflect a continuation of the expansion in output in the last quarter of 2024 as well.

тАЬAccordingly, real GDP is projected to have grown by around 5 percent in 2024, registering the highest annual growth since 2017,тАЭ Weerasinghe told the policy launching event in Colombo.

тАЬThis higher than-expected growth also provides evidence that deflation in recent months was not due to demand factors but mainly due to supply-side factors, including administrative price adjustments.тАЭ

The island nationтАЩs economy has been recovering from its worst crisis in 2022.

### No approval given for any Israeli religious centers in Sri Lanka тАУ PM

*2025-01-08 12:42:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104828/no-approval-given-for-any-israeli-religious-centers-in-sri-lanka-pm-) ┬╖ `en`

Sri LankaтАЩs Prime Minister Dr. Harini Amarasuriya stated that no government institution has so far granted authorization for the construction of Israeli religious centers or any similar places.

She made this comment in response to a question raised by SJB Member of Parliament Mujibur Rahman in Parliament today (08).

тАЬSo far, neither the Ministry of Buddhasasana, Religious and Cultural Affairs, nor any of its departments have granted permission for the construction of religious centers or similar places by Israeli nationals. However, we are aware that such centers are being maintained. We have received information about them and have observed the situation. These activities are taking place without permission, as no such approval has ever been granted,тАЭ the Prime Minister emphasized.

She further stated that they are currently discussing what actions should be taken in this regard and that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is intervening to address the issue.

The Fort MagistrateтАЩs Court has issued an order preventing the Convenor of the Inter University StudentsтАЩ Federation (IUSF), Madushan Chandrajith and others from entering the Presidential Secretariat, PresidentтАЩs House, Finance Ministry premises etc. during a planned protest in Colombo today.

Additionally, the court order restricts them from causing any inconvenience to pedestrians or vehicular traffic on several roads in Colombo, from 1.00 p.m. to 6.00 p.m. today (08).

Accordingly, this order has been issued to the convener of the IUSF, Madushan Chandrajith; the convener of the Inter-University Bhikkhu Federation (IUBF); the convener of the Medical Faculty StudentsтАЩ Action Committee, Rashmika Chamod Ranasinghe; the convener of the Student Union at the Open University in Nawala, Udara Ranasinghe; and the convener of the Faculty of Allied Health Sciences Student Union, Tharushan Piyumantha Herath.

### р╢Ер╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╢╗р╖Ъ р╢Ър╖Рр╢│р╖Ар╖Фр╢╕р╖Кр╢Ър╢╗р╖Ф р╢Зр╢нр╖Фр╖Ер╖Ф р╢┤р╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╖Гр╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╖Ьр╢зр╖Фр╖А р╢Лр╖Гр╖Пр╖Ар╖Тр╢║р╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢▒р╖Тр╢║р╖Эр╢Ьр╢║р╢Ър╖К

р╢Ер╢▒р╖Кр╢нр╢╗р╖К р╖Ар╖Тр╖Бр╖Кр╖Ар╖Ар╖Тр╢пр╖КтАНр╢║р╖Пр╢╜ р╖Бр╖Тр╖Вр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢╢р╢╜ р╢╕р╢лр╖Кр╢йр╢╜р╢║р╖Ъ р╢Ър╖Рр╢│р╖Ар╖Фр╢╕р╖Кр╢Ър╢╗р╖Ф р╢╕р╢░р╖Фр╖Вр╖Пр╢▒р╖К р╢ар╢▒р╖Кр╢пр╖КтАНр╢╗р╢вр╖Тр╢нр╖К, р╢┤р╖Фр╢вр╖КтАНр╢║ р╢╕р╖Рр╢пр╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╢Ьр╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╢║р╖Ъ р╢Йр╖Гр╖Кр╖Гр╢╗ р╢░р╢╕р╖Кр╢╕ р╖Др╖Тр╢╕р╖Т, р╢╗р╖Бр╖Кр╢╕р╖Тр╢Ъ р╢ар╢╕р╖Эр╢пр╖К р╢╗р╢лр╖Гр╖Тр╢Вр╖Д, р╢Лр╢пр╖Пр╢╗ р╢╗р╢лр╖Гр╖Тр╢Вр╖Д р╖Гр╖Д р╢нр╢╗р╖Фр╖Вр╖Пр╢▒р╖К р╢┤р╖Тр╢║р╖Фр╢╕р╢▒р╖Кр╢н р╖Др╖Ър╢╗р╢нр╖К р╢║р╢▒ р╢Ер╢║р╢з р╢╕р╖Щр╢╕ р╢▒р╖Тр╢║р╖Эр╢Ьр╢║ р╢▒р╖Тр╢Ър╖Фр╢нр╖К р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Зр╢н.

р╢Ър╖Ьр╢зр╖Фр╖А р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╢║р╖Ъ р╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╖Пр╢░р╖Тр╢┤р╢нр╖Т р╖Ар╖Тр╖Гр╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢Ер╢░р╖Тр╢Ър╢╗р╢лр╢║р╢з р╢Йр╢пр╖Тр╢╗р╖Тр╢┤р╢нр╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╜р╢п р╢Ър╢╗р╖Фр╢лр╖Ф р╖Гр╢╜р╢Ър╖П р╢╢р╖Рр╢╜р╖Тр╢╕р╖Щр╢▒р╖К р╢┤р╖Гр╖Фр╖А р╢Ер╢░р╖Тр╢Ър╢╗р╢лр╢║ р╖Ар╖Тр╖Гр╖Тр╢▒р╖К р╢Ер╢┤р╢╗р╖Пр╢░ р╢▒р╢йр╖Ф р╖Ар╖Тр╢░р╖Пр╢▒ р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ьр╖КтАНр╢╗р╢║р╢║р╖Ъ 106 (1) р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╢нр╖Тр╢┤р╖Пр╢пр╢▒ р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А р╢╕р╖Щр╢╕ р╢▒р╖Тр╢║р╖Эр╢Ьр╢║ р╢▒р╖Тр╢Ър╖Фр╢нр╖Кр╢Ър╢╗ р╢Зр╢нр╖Т р╢╢р╖А "р╢Ер╢п р╢пр╖Щр╢╗р╢л" р╢Ер╢░р╖Тр╢Ър╢╗р╢л р╖Ар╖Пр╢╗р╖Кр╢нр╖Пр╢Ър╢╗р╖Ф р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╢▒р╖К┬ар╢Ър╖Ер╖Ър╢║.

р╢Т р╢Ер╢▒р╖Фр╖А р╢Фр╖Ар╖Фр╢▒р╖Кр╢з р╢Ер╢п р╢┤р╖Гр╖Кр╖Ар╢╗р╖Ф 1:00р╢нр╖К р╖Гр╖Ар╖Г 6:00р╢нр╖К р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║ р╢нр╖Фр╖Е р╢Ър╖Ьр╢зр╖Фр╖А р╢┤р╖Ьр╢╜р╖Тр╖Гр╖К р╖Ар╖Гр╢╕р╖Ъ р╖Гр╖Щр╢╗р╢╕р╖Тр╢Ър╖К р╖Др╢Вр╢пр╖Тр╢║р╖Ъ р╖Гр╖Тр╢з NSA р╖Ар╢зр╢╗р╖Ар╖Фр╢╕ р╢пр╢Ър╖Кр╖Ар╖Пр╢п NSA р╖Ар╢зр╢╗р╖Ар╖Фр╢╕р╖Ъ р╖Гр╖Тр╢з р╢╢р╖Пр╢╜р╢пр╢Ър╖Кр╖В р╢╕р╖Пр╖Ар╢н р╢пр╢Ър╖Кр╖Ар╖П р╢Ьр╖Пр╢╜р╖Ф р╢┤р╖Пр╢╗р╢п, р╢Ер╖Ар╖Др╖Тр╢╗ р╢▒р╖Ьр╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╜р╖Щр╖Г р╢п р╢╕р╖Фр╢пр╢╜р╖К р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖КтАНр╢║р╢Вр╖Бр╢║, р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢░р╖Тр╢┤р╢нр╖Т р╢╜р╖Ър╢Ър╢╕р╖К р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖КтАНр╢║р╢╜р╢║, р╢╕р╖Д р╢╢р╖Рр╢Вр╢Ър╖Фр╖А, р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢░р╖Тр╢┤р╢нр╖Т р╢╕р╢▒р╖Кр╢пр╖Тр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╢Зр╢нр╖Фр╖Ер╖Фр╖Ар╖Тр╢╕ р╖Ар╖Ер╢Ър╖Тр╢▒ р╢╜р╖Щр╖Гр╢п р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╖Фр╢╕р╖Кр╢пр╖У р╢нр╖Тр╢╢р╖Ъ.

### 5р╖Ар╖Гр╢╗ р╖Бр╖Тр╖Вр╖КтАНр╢║р╢нр╖Кр╖А р╖Ар╖Тр╢╖р╖Пр╢Ьр╢║р╖Ъ р╢┤р╖КтАНр╢╗р╢нр╖Тр╢Ср╖Е р╢▒р╖Тр╢Ър╖Фр╢нр╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢пр╖Тр╢▒р╢║

### PM Harini stresses need for public participation in social transformation

*2025-01-08 12:05:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104826/pm-harini-stresses-need-for-public-participation-in-social-transformation) ┬╖ `en`

Prime Minister Dr. Harini Amarasuriya emphasized that changing the peopleтАЩs attitudes is essential for social transformation, and it is not a process that can be achieved overnight.

In response to a question raised in Parliament today (08) by MP Asitha Niroshana regarding how to overcome the challenges of transforming the education and media sectors, the Prime Minister stated that the citizens voted for the government to bring about a deep transformation in the country, rather than a change of individuals.

She further highlighted that public involvement is necessary for this process and stated that the government comes to power prepared to face challenges.

### Harsha proposes new regulations for тАШUndialтАЩ and тАШHawalaтАЩ systems

*2025-01-08 10:59:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104825/harsha-proposes-new-regulations-for-undial-and-hawala-systems) ┬╖ `en`

The Chairman of the Committee on Public Finance, MP Dr. Harsha de Silva stated that both the Undial system and the Hawala system are not illegal in Sri Lanka.

He made this statement while presenting several proposals in Parliament today (08).

Further commenting on the matter, he added, тАЬThe Hawala and Undial systems are not illegal in our country, but they are not regulated in any way. Therefore, a proposal has been made requiring those who conduct international transactions through these systems to register within the 12-month period from June 2024 to May 2025.тАЭ

Dr. Harsha also stated that the committee had requested the Central Bank to carry out a thorough review and submit a report on the matter. He also mentioned that the proposal had been approved and submitted to Parliament.

### тАШClean Sri LankaтАЩ programme to be debated in Parliament

*2025-01-08 10:23:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104824/clean-sri-lanka-programme-to-be-debated-in-parliament-) ┬╖ `en`

The GovernmentтАЩs тАШClean Sri LankaтАЩ national initiative is to be taken up for debate in Parliament on January 21 and 22, Prime Minister Dr. Harini Amarasuriya said in the Parliament today (08).

Prime Minister further explained that the purpose of this debate is to help the public better understand the тАШClean Sri LankaтАЩ initiative amidst the current dialogue.

### Sri Lankan insurers to tackle profitability pressure with key shifts - Fitch

*2025-01-08 10:11:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104823/sri-lankan-insurers-to-tackle-profitability-pressure-with-key-shifts-fitch) ┬╖ `en`

Underwriting profitability for Sri Lankan non-life insurers will gradually improve as they enhance practices and shift focus to more profitable non-motor segments, Fitch Ratings says in a new report.

This shift includes adjusting policy pricing, particularly for motor and medical insurance, to better cope with inflation and rising claim costs.

Motor insurance profitability faces challenges due to regulatory changes requiring full premium remittance to the National Insurance Trust Fund Board.

Non-life insurers have also been diversifying into non-motor segments such as health insurance due to prolonged import restrictions on motor vehicles.

This diversification led to an 11% increase in non-motor gross premiums in 2023.

Fitch believes that investment and liquidity risks have decreased following the upgrade of Sri LankaтАЩs sovereign rating in December 2024.

### Sri Lanka President urges withholding tax refund mechanism for retirees

*2025-01-08 10:04:00* ┬╖ [`economynextcom`](https://economynext.com/sri-lanka-president-urges-withholding-tax-refund-mechanism-for-retirees-198579/) ┬╖ `en`

ECONOMYNEXT тАУ Sri LankaтАЩs President Anura Kumara Dissanayake has discussed the setting up a mechanism of refunding withholding tax from retirees who are not subject to income tax, a statement said.

Sri Lanka is to raise withholding tax on bank deposit interest from 5 to 10 percent. Withholding tax can be set off against the final tax payment.

Income tax thresholds will also be raised from next year, reducing the total tax liability for lower income segments.

President Dissanayake had тАЬhighlighted the importance of establishing a mechanism to refund withholding taxes deducted from retirees who are not subject to income tax,тАЭ in a meeting with Finance Ministry officials, a statement from his media office said.

тАЬThe President emphasized the need for a well-balanced approach to address these concerns, taking into account the countryтАЩs financial constraints and economic priorities,тАЭ the statement said.

### Sri Lanka rupee opens slightly weaker at 296.30/50 to US dollar

*2025-01-08 09:48:00* ┬╖ [`economynextcom`](https://economynext.com/sri-lanka-rupee-opens-slightly-weaker-at-296-30-50-to-us-dollar-198577/) ┬╖ `en`

ECONOMYNEXT тАУ Sri LankaтАЩs rupee weakened to 296.20/40 to the US dollar Tuesday, dealers said with bond yields marginally higher ahead of a Treasury bill auction.

A bond maturing on 15.12.2026 was quoted at 9.40/50 percent, Wednesday down from 9.50/60 percent.

A bond maturing on 15.10.2027 was quoted at 9.80/90 percent unchanged from 9.80/95 percent.

A bond maturing on 15.02.2028 was quoted at 10.15/20 percent higher from 10.17/25 percent.

A bond maturing on 15.10.2028 was quoted at 10.50/55 percent, up from 10.45/55 percent.

A bond maturing on 01.05.2028 was quoted at 35/40 percent, steady from 10.35/42 percent.

A bond maturing on 15.09.2029 was quoted at 10.75/85 percent, unchanged.

A bond maturing on 15.05.2030 was quoted at 11.00/10 also unchanged. (Colombo/Jan7/2025)

### р╢╗р╖Ф р╢╕р╖Т 97р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Ьр╢Ър╖Ър╢▒р╖К р╢нр╖Ьр╢Ьр╢║р╢Ър╖К р╖Гр╢╕р╢Ь р╖Ар╖Тр╢пр╖Щр╖Гр╖К р╢вр╖Пр╢нр╖Тр╢Ър╢║р╖Щр╢Ър╖К р╢Ер╢нр╖Кр╢Ер╢йр╢Вр╢Ьр╖Фр╖Ар╢з

### Teacher interdicted for leaking term test questions in North Central Province

*2025-01-08 09:25:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104821/teacher-interdicted-for-leaking-term-test-questions-in-north-central-province) ┬╖ `en`

The teacher responsible for leaking the questions of the Grade 6 and 7 Term Test of government schools in North Central Province has been interdicted with immediate effect, the North Central Province Education Secretary said.

Meanwhile, on January 6, 2025, the Sinhala Literature question paper for the Grade 11 term test in the North Central Province (NCP) was leaked on social media, prompting authorities to take immediate action.

As a result, the final term test, scheduled for January 6, was postponed.

Accordingly, the distribution of the compromised question paper was halted across more than 600 schools in the province. These schools span 30 educational divisions across eight zones, according to Dharmasena.

The North Central Province Education Secretary further stated that the examination will be temporarily suspended accordingly. A new question paper will be prepared and distributed to ensure the continuation of the examination process without compromising its integrity, he noted.

### TRCSL warns public over fraudulent text messages

*2025-01-08 09:06:00* ┬╖ [`adaderanalk`](https://www.adaderana.lk/news/104819/trcsl-warns-public-over-fraudulent-text-messages) ┬╖ `en`

The Telecommunications Regulatory Commission of Sri Lanka (TRCSL) has issued a warning, advising the public not to share their personal details in response to fraudulent text messages circulating on social media.

The Commission has stated that it is receiving complaints regarding fake messages claiming that the President will offer financial assistance of Rs. 50,000 to poor families.

Accordingly, the Director of the Telecommunications Commission, Mrs. H.P.M. Pathirana, has advised individuals not to provide any personal information in response to these deceptive messages.

тАЬThe Telecommunications Regulatory Commission is receiving a large number of complaints regarding fake SMS messages. A message claiming that the President will provide Rs. 50,000 in assistance to poor families is rapidly circulating on social media networks. We request that you refrain from clicking on these links,тАЭ said the TRCSL Director.
